FNV VOLUMETRIC LOCAL-SHADOW SAMPLING CONTRACT AUDIT

Proven starting point:
1. Per-light shadow object +0x10C owns a pooled type-0x2B 1024x1024 rendered texture.
2. B9F780 renders and filters that texture; BA3390 submits the queued shadow render.
3. Selector 9 uses base_old/copy and does not prove the normal SimpleShadow consumer path.

Closure questions:
1. Which normal render path selects SimpleShadow vertex indices 89-91 and pixel indices 152-157?
2. Which texture stage receives the per-light type-0x2B texture, with what sampler/comparison state?
3. Which matrix/constant path supplies PROJ_SHADOW, and what object owns its lifetime?

Descriptor identities:
- Vertex group C: base 0x011FDE5C, count 0x67, SimpleShadow indices 89-91.
- Pixel group B: base 0x011FDB08, count 0xA0, SimpleShadow indices 152-157.
- These identities do not by themselves prove runtime selection or resource binding.
